I weeded a few of the "me too" responses and, in one case, included
someone's postscript message without also including its antecedent because
the postscript quotes the antecedent in full. (Clear?) Otherwise, the
conversation so far on ANSAX-L should be attached, in thread order,
without (alas) the trimming of extensive quotation.... The digest begins
with the context that precedes Dot's message.

If you have trouble reading the MIME digest, please let me know off-list.

Cheers,
